 main khud ko khushkismat maanata hum ki mujhe 2002 or 2006 main french neshnal squad le bluej ke saath do world cap abhiyaan kaa hissaa banane kaa mauka mila
 But my passion and love for this tournament arose long ago
 world cap ke jaadu kaa ek sira isaki shandaar viraasat se judaa he

 Become memorable
 world cap se judi meri pehali yaaden ‚Äô86 main mexico main hue mahaaayojan se judi hai

 main france main bada hua hum

 The World Cup seems like a huge celebration
 sirf media hi divaana nahin hota, balki jis tarah logon ke bich, doston-pariwaron main is par charchaa hoti rahati he, usee se pataa chalata he ki khel kitna bada he
 No matter how big your club is, our treatment of you makes you feel that your status has increased

 In a unique international competition involving 32 powerful countries from all over the world, there is a lot of tension and pressure

 The Central Reserve Bank has started communication of new currency of Rs 200 from Friday
 zyada suraksha fitures se las 200 rupee kii nai karency 8 november 2016 ko notebandi lagu hone ke baad teesri nai karency he jise bazaar main utaara ja rahaa he
 The purpose of this new currency is to remove the currency crisis arising out of currency denominations of 500 and 2000 rupees after demonetisation
 notebandi ke faisle se bazaar se 500 rupee or 1000 rupee kii karency ko hataa liya gaya tha jisaki jagah rigerv bank ne nai siries ke or adhik suraksha fitures ke 500 or 2000 rupee kii nai karency kaa sanchaar shuru kiya tha

 But the cost of printing the currency of new series of 50 and 100 rupees would have been higher, so the Reserve Bank has to normalize the market by printing more currency for less than this 200 rupee

 It is believed that due to the convenience of 2000 currency, accumulation of black money in the country has become easier and due to this there is not much communication of 2000 currency in the market
 haalanki kendriya vitt mantri arun jetali sansad main yah saaf kar chuke hai ki 2000 kii karency par kisi tarah kaa koi khatra nahin he

 1980-90 kaa dashak ek aisa vakt tha, jab is tarah kii filmein seen se ekadam hi gaayab ho gai thim
 Then only men-made films were made
 badalte daur ke saath bollywood ne bhi karavat lee he
 Now every year, a new group of new stars and directors are joining Hindi cinema
 is vajah se filmon main lagaataar nae kirdaar or nai kahaniyaan aa rahi hai
 Take Barfi (2012) as Jhilmil Chatterjee, Priyanka Chopra
 ve kisi myne main ranbir kapur se kam nahin thim

 chennai express (2013) main bhi deepika shahrukh kii takkar kii thim

 ek sensitive subject ko unhone apni acting ke jariye darshakon ke dilon ke kareeb laa diya
 Here, there is a lot of hearing about Mardani as well
 puri tasviir badal rahi he

 lekin film banane waalon ko lekar ek baat dimag main rakhana jaruri haih ham koi soshal activist nahin, ham storytailor, kahani kehane vaale log hai
 Every film we make also has a business factor
 isliye hamaari koshish complit film banane kii rahati he

 ham sirf acchhee filmein banane kii koshish kar sakate hai

 isi se inke standard kaa andaja lag jaataa he

 ek or ahm baat, hamaare yahaan quality kii bajaae quantity par zyada jor rahata he

 is trend ko badalanaa hoga

 film acchhee hogi or content solid hoga to filmein khud darshakon ko cinemagharon tak khinchengi or paise kii barish karengi
 From time to time memorable films have been made about women, including Nargis's Mother India (1957), Jaya Bhaduri's Guddi (1971) and Milli (1975), Meena Kumari's Pakija (1972), Rekha's Umrao Jaan (1981) ), Manisha Koirala's Bombay (1995) and Kajol's Dilwale Dulhania Le Jayenge (1995) are similar films
 is kadi main ham 2000 ke baad kii filmon ko dekhen to tabboo kii chandani baar (2001) or chini kam (2007), vidya baalan kii parinita (2005), paa (2009) or kahani (2012) or shridevi ke abhinay vaali meri film english winglish (2012) ko rakhaa ja saktaa he
 These are the films which portrayed the entire struggle of the woman and the whole personality in a powerful way
 idhar teen-chaar saal main ai femail actors or unki filmein ishaaron main bataa rahi hai ki aage kaa safar kaisaa rahane vaala he
 These actors are playing different types of characters on screen
 ve jindagi ko apane dhang se jeene, sirf ek aurat hone ke ehsaas se aage nikal rahi hai
 When a strong police officer is seen on the screen, a girl leaves on a honeymoon alone
 ek ladki apane shoshan ke khilaaf aawaaj uthaati he
 That is, such characters are being created for women, who are close to real life
 kul milakar film banane waalon kii soch badal rahi he
 Now women do not just come into films like show-pieces, but they have achieved their existence
 nayaa tallent ummiden jagaa rahaa he
